      <h1 class="description">
       At HealthCentral, our goal is to help you create
       <em>
        your
       </em>
       healthiest life, whatever that means in this moment. When you're living with a chronic or other serious illness, wellness doesn't fit in a tight little box. With the warmth of a friend, the authority of trusted experts, and a clear-eyed understanding of the facts, we're here to help you make informed decisions about your care with confidence—not fear.
      </h1>

  function modifyOsanoBanner() {
    try {
      var osanoEl = document.querySelector('.osano-cm-dialog');

      if (!osanoEl) {
        return;
      }

      var topIt = document.location.search.toLowerCase().indexOf('ap=tegnacustom') !== -1;

      if (topIt) {
        osanoEl.classList.add('rhm-osano-cm-dialog--position');
        osanoEl.classList.remove('osano-cm-dialog--position_bottom');
      }

      var osanoBtns = document.querySelector('.osano-cm-buttons');

      if (osanoBtns === null) {
        var closer = document.createElement('DIV');
        closer.style = 'display: block; width: 20px; height: 20px; line-height: 20px; text-align: center; font-size:12px; background-color:#494B4D; color:#fff; border-radius: 50%; cursor: pointer; position: absolute; top: 8px; right: 8px;';
        closer.innerHTML = '<span onclick="closeOsanoDialog()">&#10005;</span>';
        osanoEl.appendChild(closer);
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  }

        modifyOsanoBanner();
      }
